```python
        Konstrikt√® pou Fichier
        
        Args:
            non (str): Non fichier la
            gwos√® (int): Gwos√® fichier la nan bytes
        """
        self.non = non
        self.gwos√® = gwos√®
        self.ouvri = False
        print(f"Fichier '{self.non}' kreye ({self.gwos√®} bytes)")
    
    def ouvri_fichier(self):
        """
        Ouvri fichier la
        """
        if not self.ouvri:
            self.ouvri = True
            print(f"Fichier '{self.non}' ouvri")
        else:
            print(f"Fichier '{self.non}' deja ouvri")
    
    def f√®men_fichier(self):
        """
        F√®men fichier la
        """
        if self.ouvri:
            self.ouvri = False
            print(f"Fichier '{self.non}' f√®men")
        else:
            print(f"Fichier '{self.non}' deja f√®men")
    
    def __del__(self):
        """
        Destrikt√® - Netwaye resous yo
        """
        if self.ouvri:
            print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è Fichier '{self.non}' pa t f√®men! F√®men li...")
            self.f√®men_fichier()
        print(f"Fichier '{self.non}' detwi")
    
    def __str__(self):
        """
        Reprezantasyon string pou Fichier
        """
        eta = "ouvri" if self.ouvri else "f√®men"
        return f"Fichier: {self.non} ({self.gwos√®} bytes, {eta})"
    
    def __repr__(self):
        """
        Reprezantasyon teknik pou Fichier
        """
        return f"Fichier('{self.non}', {self.gwos√®})"

# Kreye fichier yo
fichier1 = Fichier("dokiman.txt", 1024)
fichier2 = Fichier("imaj.jpg", 2048)

# S√®vi ak fichier yo
fichier1.ouvri_fichier()
fichier2.ouvri_fichier()
fichier1.f√®men_fichier()

# Afiche enf√≤masyon yo
print(f"Fichier 1: {fichier1}")
print(f"Fichier 2: {fichier2}")

# Detwi fichier yo (destrikt√® yo pral rele)
del fichier1
del fichier2
```

**Egzanp 2: Met√≤d Espesyal Konpl√®ks**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 2: MET√íD ESPESYAL KONPL√àKS ===")

class Vekt√®:
    """
    Klas pou reprezante yon vekt√® 2D
    """
    
    def __init__(self, x, y):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Vekt√®
        
        Args:
            x (float): K√≤√≤done x
            y (float): K√≤√≤done y
        """
        self.x = x
        self.y = y
    
    def __str__(self):
        """
        Reprezantasyon string pou Vekt√®
        """
        return f"Vekt√®({self.x}, {self.y})"
    
    def __repr__(self):
        """
        Reprezantasyon teknik pou Vekt√®
        """
        return f"Vekt√®({self.x}, {self.y})"
    
    def __add__(self, l√≤t):
        """
        Adisyon de vekt√®
        
        Args:
            l√≤t (Vekt√®): L√≤t vekt√® pou ajoute
        
        Returns:
            Vekt√®: Nouvo vekt√®
        """
        return Vekt√®(self.x + l√≤t.x, self.y + l√≤t.y)
    
    def __sub__(self, l√≤t):
        """
        Soustraksyon de vekt√®
        
        Args:
            l√≤t (Vekt√®): L√≤t vekt√® pou soustraksyon
        
        Returns:
            Vekt√®: Nouvo vekt√®
        """
        return Vekt√®(self.x - l√≤t.x, self.y - l√≤t.y)
    
    def __mul__(self, skalar):
        """
        Miltiplikasyon vekt√® ak skalar
        
        Args:
            skalar (float): Nimewo pou miltipliye
        
        Returns:
            Vekt√®: Nouvo vekt√®
        """
        return Vekt√®(self.x * skalar, self.y * skalar)
    
    def __len__(self):
        """
        Long√® vekt√® a (magnitude)
        
        Returns:
            float: Long√® vekt√® a
        """
        import math
        return math.sqrt(self.x**2 + self.y**2)
    
    def __eq__(self, l√≤t):
        """
        Konparezon egalite
        
        Args:
            l√≤t (Vekt√®): L√≤t vekt√® pou konpare
        
        Returns:
            bool: True si egal, False sinon
        """
        return self.x == l√≤t.x and self.y == l√≤t.y

# Teste vekt√® yo
v1 = Vekt√®(3, 4)
v2 = Vekt√®(1, 2)

print(f"V1: {v1}")
print(f"V2: {v2}")
print(f"V1 + V2: {v1 + v2}")
print(f"V1 - V2: {v1 - v2}")
print(f"V1 * 2: {v1 * 2}")
print(f"Long√® V1: {len(v1):.2f}")
print(f"V1 == V2: {v1 == v2}")
```

---

### üîß Met√≤d Static, Instance, ak Class

#### üéØ Kisa se "Met√≤d Static, Instance, ak Class"?

**Instance Method** se met√≤d ki travay ak obj√® espesifik.
**Static Method** se met√≤d ki pa bezwen obj√® pou travay.
**Class Method** se met√≤d ki travay ak klas la menm.

> **üí° TIP:** Instance se tankou aksyon yon moun espesifik, static se tankou aksyon jeneral, class se tankou aksyon pou tout moun nan yon gwoup.

#### üìã Kalite Met√≤d

| Kalite | Deskripsyon | Sentaks |
|--------|-------------|---------|
| **Instance** | Travay ak obj√® espesifik | `def met√≤d(self):` |
| **Static** | Pa bezwen obj√® | `@staticmethod` |
| **Class** | Travay ak klas | `@classmethod` |

#### üîß Egzanp Detaye Kalite Met√≤d

**Egzanp 1: Met√≤d Instance**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 1: MET√íD INSTANCE ===")

class El√®v:
    """
    Klas pou reprezante yon el√®v
    """
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou El√®v
        
        Args:
            non (str): Non el√®v la
            laj (int): Laj el√®v la
        """
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
        self.n√≤t_yo = []
    
    def ajoute_n√≤t(self, n√≤t):
        """
        Met√≤d instance - ajoute n√≤t pou el√®v espesifik
        
        Args:
            n√≤t (float): N√≤t pou ajoute
        """
        self.n√≤t_yo.append(n√≤t)
        print(f"N√≤t {n√≤t} ajoute pou {self.non}")
    
    def kalkile_mway√®n(self):
        """
        Met√≤d instance - kalkile mway√®n pou el√®v espesifik
        
        Returns:
            float: Mway√®n n√≤t yo
        """
        if self.n√≤t_yo:
            return sum(self.n√≤t_yo) / len(self.n√≤t_yo)
        return 0.0
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Met√≤d instance - afiche enf√≤masyon el√®v espesifik
        """
        print(f"El√®v: {self.non}, Laj: {self.laj}")
        print(f"N√≤t yo: {self.n√≤t_yo}")
        print(f"Mway√®n: {self.kalkile_mway√®n():.2f}")

# Kreye el√®v yo
el√®v1 = El√®v("Marie", 15)
el√®v2 = El√®v("Jean", 16)

# S√®vi ak met√≤d instance
el√®v1.ajoute_n√≤t(85)
el√®v1.ajoute_n√≤t(90)
el√®v1.afiche_inf√≤()

el√®v2.ajoute_n√≤t(78)
el√®v2.ajoute_n√≤t(92)
el√®v2.afiche_inf√≤()
```

**Egzanp 2: Met√≤d Static**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 2: MET√íD STATIC ===")

class Matematik:
    """
    Klas pou fonksyon matematik
    """
    
    @staticmethod
    def kalkile_kare(nimewo):
        """
        Met√≤d static - kalkile kare yon nimewo
        
        Args:
            nimewo (float): Nimewo pou kalkile kare
        
        Returns:
            float: Kare nimewo a
        """
        return nimewo ** 2
    
    @staticmethod
    def kalkile_kib(nimewo):
        """
        Met√≤d static - kalkile kib yon nimewo
        
        Args:
            nimewo (float): Nimewo pou kalkile kib
        
        Returns:
            float: Kib nimewo a
        """
        return nimewo ** 3
    
    @staticmethod
    def teste_nimewo_premye(nimewo):
        """
        Met√≤d static - teste si yon nimewo se premye
        
        Args:
            nimewo (int): Nimewo pou teste
        
        Returns:
            bool: True si premye, False sinon
        """
        if nimewo < 2:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(nimewo**0.5) + 1):
            if nimewo % i == 0:
                return False
        return True
    
    @staticmethod
    def jenere_lis_nimewo_premye(limit):
        """
        Met√≤d static - jenere lis nimewo premye
        
        Args:
            limit (int): Limit pou jenere
        
        Returns:
            list: Lis nimewo premye yo
        """
        premye_yo = []
        for n in range(2, limit + 1):
            if Matematik.teste_nimewo_premye(n):
                premye_yo.append(n)
        return premye_yo

# S√®vi ak met√≤d static
print(f"Kare 5: {Matematik.kalkile_kare(5)}")
print(f"Kib 3: {Matematik.kalkile_kib(3)}")
print(f"7 se premye: {Matematik.teste_nimewo_premye(7)}")
print(f"8 se premye: {Matematik.teste_nimewo_premye(8)}")
print(f"Nimewo premye jiska 20: {Matematik.jenere_lis_nimewo_premye(20)}")
```

**Egzanp 3: Met√≤d Class**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 3: MET√íD CLASS ===")

class P√®son:
    """
    Klas pou reprezante yon p√®son
    """
    
    total_p√®son = 0  # Varyab klas
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou P√®son
        
        Args:
            non (str): Non p√®son nan
            laj (int): Laj p√®son nan
        """
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
        P√®son.total_p√®son += 1
    
    @classmethod
    def kreye_ak_enf√≤(cls, enf√≤masyon):
        """
        Met√≤d class - kreye p√®son ak enf√≤masyon
        
        Args:
            enf√≤masyon (str): Enf√≤masyon nan f√≤ma "non,laj"
        
        Returns:
            P√®son: Nouvo p√®son
        """
        non, laj = enf√≤masyon.split(',')
        return cls(non.strip(), int(laj.strip()))
    
    @classmethod
    def kreye_ak_laj_defo(cls, non):
        """
        Met√≤d class - kreye p√®son ak laj defo
        
        Args:
            non (str): Non p√®son nan
        
        Returns:
            P√®son: Nouvo p√®son
        """
        return cls(non, 18)  # Laj defo 18
    
    @classmethod
    def afiche_total(cls):
        """
        Met√≤d class - afiche total p√®son yo
        
        Returns:
            int: Total p√®son yo
        """
        print(f"Total p√®son yo: {cls.total_p√®son}")
        return cls.total_p√®son
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Met√≤d instance - afiche enf√≤masyon p√®son nan
        """
        print(f"Non: {self.non}, Laj: {self.laj}")

# S√®vi ak met√≤d class
p√®son1 = P√®son("Marie", 25)
p√®son2 = P√®son.kreye_ak_enf√≤("Jean, 30")
p√®son3 = P√®son.kreye_ak_laj_defo("Sara")

# Afiche enf√≤masyon yo
p√®son1.afiche_inf√≤()
p√®son2.afiche_inf√≤()
p√®son3.afiche_inf√≤()

# Afiche total
P√®son.afiche_total()
```

---

### üîß Eritaj (Inheritance)

#### üéØ Kisa se "Eritaj"?

**Eritaj** se fason yon klas ka herite karakteristik ak met√≤d nan yon l√≤t klas. Li p√®m√®t ou kreye klas nouvo ki bati sou klas ki deja egziste.

> **üí° TIP:** Eritaj se tankou yon fanmi - timoun yo herite karakteristik nan paran yo men yo ka genyen karakteristik espesyal tou.

#### üìã Sentaks Eritaj

```python
class KlasParent:
    """
    Klas parent
    """
    pass

class KlasChild(KlasParent):
    """
    Klas child ki herite nan KlasParent
    """
    pass
```

#### üîß Egzanp Detaye Eritaj

**Egzanp 1: Eritaj Debaz**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 1: ERITAJ DEBAZ ===")

class Animal:
    """
    Klas parent pou tout b√®t yo
    """
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Animal
        
        Args:
            non (str): Non b√®t la
            laj (int): Laj b√®t la
        """
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
    
    def manje(self):
        """
        Met√≤d pou manje
        """
        print(f"{self.non} ap manje")
    
    def d√≤mi(self):
        """
        Met√≤d pou d√≤mi
        """
        print(f"{self.non} ap d√≤mi")
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Afiche enf√≤masyon b√®t la
        """
        print(f"Non: {self.non}, Laj: {self.laj}")

class Chen(Animal):
    """
    Klas child pou chen yo
    """
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj, ras):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Chen
        
        Args:
            non (str): Non chen an
            laj (int): Laj chen an
            ras (str): Ras chen an
        """
        super().__init__(non, laj)  # Rele konstrikt√® parent
        self.ras = ras
    
    def abw√®(self):
        """
        Met√≤d espesyal pou chen
        """
        print(f"{self.non} ap abw√®: Woof! Woof!")
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Afiche enf√≤masyon chen an
        """
        super().afiche_inf√≤()  # Rele met√≤d parent
        print(f"Ras: {self.ras}")

class Chat(Animal):
    """
    Klas child pou chat yo
    """
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj, koul√®):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Chat
        
        Args:
            non (str): Non chat la
            laj (int): Laj chat la
            koul√® (str): Koul√® chat la
        """
        super().__init__(non, laj)  # Rele konstrikt√® parent
        self.koul√® = koul√®
    
    def miyaw(self):
        """
        Met√≤d espesyal pou chat
        """
        print(f"{self.non} ap miyaw: Meow! Meow!")
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Afiche enf√≤masyon chat la
        """
        super().afiche_inf√≤()  # Rele met√≤d parent
        print(f"Koul√®: {self.koul√®}")

# Kreye b√®t yo
chen1 = Chen("Rex", 3, "German Shepherd")
chat1 = Chat("Whiskers", 2, "Nwa")

# S√®vi ak met√≤d yo
chen1.afiche_inf√≤()
chen1.manje()
chen1.abw√®()

print()

chat1.afiche_inf√≤()
chat1.d√≤mi()
chat1.miyaw()
```

**Egzanp 2: Eritaj Konpl√®ks**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 2: ERITAJ KONPL√àKS ===")

class Veyikil:
    """
    Klas parent pou tout veyikil yo
    """
    
    def __init__(self, mak, mod√®l, ane):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Veyikil
        
        Args:
            mak (str): Mak veyikil la
            mod√®l (str): Mod√®l veyikil la
            ane (int): Ane veyikil la
        """
        self.mak = mak
        self.mod√®l = mod√®l
        self.ane = ane
        self.vit√®s = 0
    
    def demare(self):
        """
        Demare veyikil la
        """
        print(f"{self.mak} {self.mod√®l} demare")
        self.vit√®s = 10
    
    def rale(self):
        """
        Rale veyikil la
        """
        print(f"{self.mak} {self.mod√®l} rale")
        self.vit√®s = 0
    
    def akselere(self, kantite):
        """
        Akselere veyikil la
        
        Args:
            kantite (int): Kantite pou akselere
        """
        self.vit√®s += kantite
        print(f"{self.mak} {self.mod√®l} akselere nan {self.vit√®s} km/h")
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Afiche enf√≤masyon veyikil la
        """
        print(f"Veyikil: {self.mak} {self.mod√®l} ({self.ane})")
        print(f"Vit√®s akty√®l: {self.vit√®s} km/h")

class Machin(Veyikil):
    """
    Klas child pou machin yo
    """
    
    def __init__(self, mak, mod√®l, ane, nimewo_siye):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Machin
        
        Args:
            mak (str): Mak machin nan
            mod√®l (str): Mod√®l machin nan
            ane (int): Ane machin nan
            nimewo_siye (str): Nimewo siye machin nan
        """
        super().__init__(mak, mod√®l, ane)
        self.nimewo_siye = nimewo_siye
        self.nimewo_pasaj√® = 0
    
    def monte_pasaj√®(self, kantite):
        """
        Monte pasaj√® nan machin nan
        
        Args:
            kantite (int): Kantite pasaj√® pou monte
        """
        self.nimewo_pasaj√® += kantite
        print(f"{kantite} pasaj√® monte nan machin nan")
    
    def desann_pasaj√®(self, kantite):
        """
        Desann pasaj√® nan machin nan
        
        Args:
            kantite (int): Kantite pasaj√® pou desann
        """
        if kantite <= self.nimewo_pasaj√®:
            self.nimewo_pasaj√® -= kantite
            print(f"{kantite} pasaj√® desann nan machin nan")
        else:
            print("Pa gen ase pasaj√® nan machin nan")
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Afiche enf√≤masyon machin nan
        """
        super().afiche_inf√≤()
        print(f"Nimewo siye: {self.nimewo_siye}")
        print(f"Pasaj√® yo: {self.nimewo_pasaj√®}")

class Motosikl√®t(Veyikil):
    """
    Klas child pou motosikl√®t yo
    """
    
    def __init__(self, mak, mod√®l, ane, gwos√®_mot√®):
        """
        Konstrikt√® pou Motosikl√®t
        
        Args:
            mak (str): Mak motosikl√®t la
            mod√®l (str): Mod√®l motosikl√®t la
            ane (int): Ane motosikl√®t la
            gwos√®_mot√® (int): Gwos√® mot√® a nan cc
        """
        super().__init__(mak, mod√®l, ane)
        self.gwos√®_mot√® = gwos√®_mot√®
        self.kaske = False
    
    def mete_kaske(self):
        """
        Mete kaske
        """
        self.kaske = True
        print("Kaske mete")
    
    def retire_kaske(self):
        """
        Retire kaske
        """
        self.kaske = False
        print("Kaske retire")
    
    def akselere(self, kantite):
        """
        Akselere motosikl√®t la (ovrride met√≤d parent)
        
        Args:
            kantite (int): Kantite pou akselere
        """
        if not self.kaske:
            print("‚ö†Ô∏è Mete kaske anvan ou akselere!")
            return
        
        super().akselere(kantite)
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """
        Afiche enf√≤masyon motosikl√®t la
        """
        super().afiche_inf√≤()
        print(f"Gwos√® mot√®: {self.gwos√®_mot√®}cc")
        print(f"Kaske: {'Mete' if self.kaske else 'Pa mete'}")

# Kreye veyikil yo
machin1 = Machin("Toyota", "Camry", 2020, "ABC-123")
motosikl√®t1 = Motosikl√®t("Honda", "CBR", 2021, 600)

# S√®vi ak machin nan
machin1.demare()
machin1.monte_pasaj√®(3)
machin1.akselere(30)
machin1.afiche_inf√≤()

print()

# S√®vi ak motosikl√®t la
motosikl√®t1.demare()
motosikl√®t1.mete_kaske()
motosikl√®t1.akselere(50)
motosikl√®t1.afiche_inf√≤()
```

---

### üìä Resime Klas ak Obj√®

#### üéØ T√®m Enp√≤tan yo

| T√®m | Deskripsyon | Egzanp |
|-----|-------------|---------|
| **Class** | Plan pou kreye obj√® | `class P√®son:` |
| **Object** | Egzanp yon klas | `p√®son1 = P√®son()` |
| **Constructor** | Inisyalize obj√® | `def __init__(self):` |
| **Method** | Fonksyon nan klas | `def met√≤d(self):` |
| **Attribute** | Karakteristik obj√® | `self.non = "Marie"` |
| **Inheritance** | Herite nan klas parent | `class Child(Parent):` |
| **Encapsulation** | Kache detay ent√®n | `self.__private` |
| **Polymorphism** | Yon menm aksyon, diferan rezilta | Override met√≤d |

#### üîß R√®g Enp√≤tan

1. **Naming**: Non klas yo dwe k√≤manse ak l√®t majiskil
2. **Constructor**: Toujou defini `__init__` si neses√®
3. **Self**: Toujou s√®vi ak `self` nan met√≤d instance
4. **Inheritance**: S√®vi ak `super()` pou rele met√≤d parent
5. **Documentation**: Toujou ekri docstring

#### ‚ö†Ô∏è Er√® Komen

1. **Oubliye self** nan met√≤d instance
2. **Pa rele super()** nan konstrikt√® child
3. **Pa respekte naming** konvansyon yo
4. **Pa teste klas** yo ak diferan obj√®

---

### üéÆ Egz√®sis Pratik

**Egz√®sis 1: Klas Bank**
Kreye yon klas Bank ak met√≤d pou jere kont yo.

**Egz√®sis 2: Klas Lek√≤l**
Kreye yon klas Lek√≤l ak eritaj pou El√®v ak Pwofes√®.

**Egz√®sis 3: Klas Jw√®t**
Kreye yon klas Jw√®t ak eritaj pou diferan kalite jw√®t.

**Egz√®sis 4: Sist√®m Bibliyot√®k**
Kreye yon sist√®m jesyon bibliyot√®k ak OOP.
2. **Reutilizasyon**: S√®vi ak menm k√≤d la plizy√® fwa
3. **Kenbe**: Pi fasil pou chanje ak amelyore
4. **Entelijan**: K√≤d la imite reyalite a
5. **Evolisyon**: Pi fasil pou ajoute nouvo karakteristik

**Analoji ki fasil konprann:**
- **Klas** = Tankou yon plan pou yon machin
- **Obj√®** = Tankou machin rey√®l yo ki f√®t dapre plan an
- **Atribi** = Karakteristik yo (koul√®, gwos√®, etc.)
- **Met√≤d** = Aksyon yo ka f√® (kondwi, frene, etc.)

### üîß T√®m Fondamantal nan OOP

#### 1. **Class** (Klas) - Plan Pou Kreye Obj√®

**Kisa se "Class"?**

**Class** se yon plan oswa mod√®l pou kreye obj√®. Li defini ki karakteristik ak aksyon obj√® yo pral genyen.

**Poukisa Class Enp√≤tan?**
- Li se plan nan pou kreye obj√® yo
- Li defini tout karakteristik ak aksyon yo
- Ou ka kreye plizy√® obj√® dapre menm plan an

**Egzanp Class:**
```python
class El√®v:
    """Klas El√®v - Plan pou kreye el√®v yo"""
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj, klas):
        """Konstrikt√® - Kreye yon el√®v nouvo"""
        self.non = non        # Atribi: non el√®v la
        self.laj = laj        # Atribi: laj el√®v la
        self.klas = klas      # Atribi: klas el√®v la
        self.n√≤t_yo = []      # Atribi: lis n√≤t el√®v la
```

**R√®g Class:**
- K√≤manse ak mo kle `class`
- Non klas la dwe k√≤manse ak l√®t majiskil
- Chak klas gen karakteristik ak aksyon

#### 2. **Object** (Obj√®) - Eksempl√® Rey√®l

**Kisa se "Object"?**

**Object** se yon eksempl√® rey√®l ki f√®t dapre yon klas. Li se tankou yon machin rey√®l ki f√®t dapre plan machin an.

**Poukisa Object Enp√≤tan?**
- Sa se bagay rey√®l la ke ou s√®vi
- Chak obj√® gen enf√≤masyon ak aksyon pa li
- Ou ka kreye plizy√® obj√® dapre menm klas la

**Egzanp Object:**
```python
# Kreye obj√® yo dapre klas El√®v
marie = El√®v("Marie", 20, "3e ane")    # Obj√®: marie
jean = El√®v("Jean", 19, "2e ane")      # Obj√®: jean
sara = El√®v("Sara", 21, "4e ane")      # Obj√®: sara
```

#### 3. **Constructor** (Konstrikt√®) - Fonkisyon Kreasyon

**Kisa se "Constructor"?**

**Constructor** se yon fonksyon espesyal nan yon klas ki rele otomatikman l√® ou kreye yon nouvo obj√®. Li se tankou yon chef ki prepare yon plat nouvo.

**Poukisa Constructor Enp√≤tan?**
- Li prepare nouvo obj√® a
- Li bay val√® inisyal pou atribi yo
- Li rele otomatikman l√® obj√® a kreye

**Egzanp Constructor:**
```python
def __init__(self, non, laj, klas):
    """Konstrikt√® - Prepare nouvo el√®v la"""
    print(f"Kreye el√®v: {non}")
    self.non = non        # Bay non el√®v la
    self.laj = laj        # Bay laj el√®v la
    self.klas = klas      # Bay klas el√®v la
    self.n√≤t_yo = []      # K√≤manse ak lis n√≤t vid
```

**R√®g Constructor:**
- Non li se toujou `__init__`
- Premye param√®t li se toujou `self`
- Li rele otomatikman l√® obj√® a kreye

#### 4. **self** - Referans Obj√®

**Kisa se "self"?**

**self** se referans nan obj√® akty√®l la nan yon klas. Li se tankou di "mwen menm" nan yon konv√®sasyon.

**Poukisa self Enp√≤tan?**
- Li di Python ki obj√® ou ap travay ak
- Li p√®m√®t aks√® atribi ak met√≤d obj√® a
- Chak obj√® gen `self` pa li

**Egzanp self:**
```python
def ajoute_n√≤t(self, n√≤t):
    """Ajoute n√≤t nan lis el√®v la"""
    self.n√≤t_yo.append(n√≤t)    # self.n√≤t_yo = n√≤t yo nan obj√® sa a
    print(f"{self.non} jwenn n√≤t: {n√≤t}")  # self.non = non obj√® sa a
```

#### 5. **Attribute** (Atribi) - Karakteristik Obj√®

**Kisa se "Attribute"?**

**Attribute** se yon karakteristik ke yon obj√® genyen. Li se tankou yon karakteristik ke yon moun genyen (non, laj, wot√®, etc.).

**Poukisa Attribute Enp√≤tan?**
- Yo defini karakteristik obj√® a
- Chak obj√® gen atribi pa li
- Ou ka chanje atribi yo

**Egzanp Attribute:**
```python
class El√®v:
    def __init__(self, non, laj, klas):
        self.non = non        # Atribi: non el√®v la
        self.laj = laj        # Atribi: laj el√®v la
        self.klas = klas      # Atribi: klas el√®v la
        self.n√≤t_yo = []      # Atribi: lis n√≤t el√®v la
        self.prezan = True    # Atribi: si el√®v la prezan

# Aksede atribi yo
print(marie.non)          # Afiche non el√®v la
print(marie.laj)          # Afiche laj el√®v la
print(marie.klas)         # Afiche klas el√®v la
```

#### 6. **Method** (Met√≤d) - Aksyon Obj√®

**Kisa se "Method"?**

**Method** se yon fonksyon ke yon obj√® ka s√®vi. Li se tankou yon aksyon ke yon moun ka f√® (kondwi, manje, d√≤mi, etc.).

**Poukisa Method Enp√≤tan?**
- Yo defini aksyon obj√® a ka f√®
- Chak obj√® ka s√®vi ak met√≤d yo
- Yo √≤ganize aksyon yo nan klas la

**Egzanp Method:**
```python
def ajoute_n√≤t(self, n√≤t):
    """Met√≤d: Ajoute yon n√≤t nan lis el√®v la"""
    self.n√≤t_yo.append(n√≤t)
    print(f"{self.non} jwenn n√≤t: {n√≤t}")

def kalkile_mway√®n(self):
    """Met√≤d: Kalkile n√≤t mway√®n el√®v la"""
    if len(self.n√≤t_yo) == 0:
        return 0
    mway√®n = sum(self.n√≤t_yo) / len(self.n√≤t_yo)
    print(f"{self.non} gen mway√®n: {mway√®n:.2f}")
    return mway√®n

def afiche_inf√≤(self):
    """Met√≤d: Afiche tout enf√≤masyon el√®v la"""
    print(f"Non: {self.non}")
    print(f"Laj: {self.laj}")
    print(f"Klas: {self.klas}")
    print(f"Mway√®n: {self.kalkile_mway√®n():.2f}")
```

#### 7. **Instance** (Eksempl√®) - Obj√® Rey√®l

**Kisa se "Instance"?**

**Instance** se yon l√≤t mo pou "obj√®" - li se yon eksempl√® rey√®l ki f√®t dapre yon klas.

**Egzanp Instance:**
```python
marie = El√®v("Marie", 20, "3e ane")    # marie se yon instance
jean = El√®v("Jean", 19, "2e ane")      # jean se yon instance
sara = El√®v("Sara", 21, "4e ane")      # sara se yon instance
```

#### 8. **Encapsulation** (Enkapsulasyon) - Kache Detay

**Kisa se "Encapsulation"?**

**Encapsulation** se prensip pou kache detay ent√®n yo ak s√®lman montre sa ki neses√®. Li se tankou yon machin - ou pa bezwen konnen kijan mot√® a travay, ou s√®lman bezwen konnen kijan kondwi.

**Egzanp Encapsulation:**
```python
class El√®v:
    def __init__(self, non, laj, klas):
        self.non = non        # Piblik - tout moun ka w√®
        self.laj = laj        # Piblik - tout moun ka w√®
        self._klas = klas     # Pwot√®je - s√®lman klas la ka w√®
        self.__n√≤t_yo = []    # Prive - pa gen moun ka w√®

    def ajoute_n√≤t(self, n√≤t):
        """Met√≤d piblik - tout moun ka s√®vi"""
        self.__n√≤t_yo.append(n√≤t)

    def _met√≤d_pwot√®je(self):
        """Met√≤d pwot√®je - s√®lman klas la ka s√®vi"""
        pass

    def __met√≤d_prive(self):
        """Met√≤d prive - pa gen moun ka s√®vi"""
        pass
```

#### 9. **Inheritance** (Eritaj) - Herite Karakteristik

**Kisa se "Inheritance"?**

**Inheritance** se prensip pou yon klas ka herite karakteristik ak aksyon nan yon l√≤t klas. Li se tankou yon timoun ki herite karakteristik nan paran li yo.

**Egzanp Inheritance:**
```python
class P√®son:
    """Klas paran - karakteristik komen"""
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
    
    def di_bonjou(self):
        print(f"Bonjou! Mwen rele {self.non}")

class El√®v(P√®son):  # El√®v herite nan P√®son
    """Klas pitit - karakteristik espesifik"""
    def __init__(self, non, laj, klas):
        super().__init__(non, laj)  # Rele konstrikt√® paran an
        self.klas = klas
        self.n√≤t_yo = []
    
    def etidye(self):
        print(f"{self.non} ap etidye nan klas {self.klas}")

class Pwofes√®(P√®son):  # Pwofes√® herite nan P√®son
    """Klas pitit - karakteristik espesifik"""
    def __init__(self, non, laj, maty√®):
        super().__init__(non, laj)  # Rele konstrikt√® paran an
        self.maty√® = maty√®
    
    def anseye(self):
        print(f"{self.non} ap anseye {self.maty√®}")
```

#### 10. **Polymorphism** (Polim√≤fis) - Plizy√® F√≤m

**Kisa se "Polymorphism"?**

**Polymorphism** se prensip pou obj√® diferan ka s√®vi ak menm met√≤d la nan fason diferan. Li se tankou diferan kalite b√®t ki ka kouri, men chak yon s√®vi nan fason pa li.

**Egzanp Polymorphism:**
```python
class B√®t:
    def kouri(self):
        print("B√®t la ap kouri")

class Chyen(B√®t):
    def kouri(self):
        print("Chyen an ap kouri ak pat li yo")

class Chat(B√®t):
    def kouri(self):
        print("Chat la ap kouri ak pat li yo")

class Lapen(B√®t):
    def kouri(self):
        print("Lapen an ap sote ak pat li yo")

# Polymorphism - menm met√≤d, diferan aksyon
b√®t_yo = [Chyen(), Chat(), Lapen()]

for b√®t in b√®t_yo:
    b√®t.kouri()  # Chak b√®t kouri nan fason pa li
```

### üéÆ Egzanp Pratik Konpl√®

```python
# üéÆ EGZANP AMIZAN: Ou nan yon lek√≤l ak el√®v yo

print("üè´ SITUASYON: Ou nan yon lek√≤l ak el√®v yo")
print("=" * 45)

# 1. KREYE KLAS EL√àV
print("1Ô∏è‚É£ KREYE KLAS EL√àV")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'F√® plan pou yon el√®v'")

class El√®v:
    """Klas El√®v - Plan pou kreye el√®v yo"""
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj, klas):
        """Konstrikt√® - Kreye yon el√®v nouvo"""
        print(f"   üéì Kreye el√®v: {non}")
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
        self.klas = klas
        self.n√≤t_yo = []
        self.prezan = True
    
    def ajoute_n√≤t(self, n√≤t):
        """Ajoute yon n√≤t nan lis el√®v la"""
        print(f"   üìä {self.non} jwenn n√≤t: {n√≤t}")
        self.n√≤t_yo.append(n√≤t)
    
    def kalkile_mway√®n(self):
        """Kalkile n√≤t mway√®n el√®v la"""
        if len(self.n√≤t_yo) == 0:
            return 0
        mway√®n = sum(self.n√≤t_yo) / len(self.n√≤t_yo)
        print(f"   üìà {self.non} gen mway√®n: {mway√®n:.2f}")
        return mway√®n
    
    def afiche_inf√≤(self):
        """Afiche tout enf√≤masyon el√®v la"""
        print(f"   üë§ Non: {self.non}")
        print(f"   üéÇ Laj: {self.laj} an")
        print(f"   üè´ Klas: {self.klas}")
        print(f"   üìä N√≤t yo: {self.n√≤t_yo}")
        print(f"   üìà Mway√®n: {self.kalkile_mway√®n():.2f}")
        print(f"   ‚úÖ Prezan: {self.prezan}")
        print()
    
    def chanje_klas(self, nouvo_klas):
        """Chanje klas el√®v la"""
        ansyen_klas = self.klas
        self.klas = nouvo_klas
        print(f"   üîÑ {self.non} chanje klas: {ansyen_klas} ‚Üí {nouvo_klas}")
    
    def f√®_aniv√®s√®(self):
        """El√®v la f√® aniv√®s√® li"""
        self.laj += 1
        print(f"   üéâ {self.non} f√® {self.laj} an! Bon aniv√®s√®!")

print("   üìã Klas El√®v kreye ak siks√®!")
print()

# 2. KREYE OBJ√à YO
print("2Ô∏è‚É£ KREYE OBJ√à YO")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'F√® el√®v rey√®l yo dapre plan an'")

print("üìö Kreye el√®v yo:")
marie = El√®v("Marie", 20, "3e ane")
jean = El√®v("Jean", 19, "2e ane")
sara = El√®v("Sara", 21, "4e ane")

print()

# 3. S√àVI AK OBJ√à YO
print("3Ô∏è‚É£ S√àVI AK OBJ√à YO")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'F√® aksyon ak el√®v yo'")

# Ajoute n√≤t yo
print("üìä Ajoute n√≤t yo:")
marie.ajoute_n√≤t(15)
marie.ajoute_n√≤t(18)
marie.ajoute_n√≤t(20)

jean.ajoute_n√≤t(12)
jean.ajoute_n√≤t(16)
jean.ajoute_n√≤t(18)

sara.ajoute_n√≤t(19)
sara.ajoute_n√≤t(17)
sara.ajoute_n√≤t(21)

print()

# Afiche enf√≤masyon yo
print("üìã Afiche enf√≤masyon yo:")
marie.afiche_inf√≤()
jean.afiche_inf√≤()
sara.afiche_inf√≤()

# F√® aksyon yo
print("üéØ F√® aksyon yo:")
marie.chanje_klas("4e ane")
marie.f√®_aniv√®s√®()

jean.chanje_klas("3e ane")

sara.f√®_aniv√®s√®()

print()

# 4. AKS√àDE ATRIBƒ∞ YO
print("4Ô∏è‚É£ AKS√àDE ATRIBƒ∞ YO")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'Jwenn enf√≤masyon nan obj√® yo'")

print(f"   üìù Non Marie: {marie.non}")
print(f"   üéÇ Laj Jean: {jean.laj}")
print(f"   üè´ Klas Sara: {sara.klas}")
print(f"   üìä N√≤t Marie: {marie.n√≤t_yo}")

print()

print("üéâ BRAVO! Ou konprann KLAS ak OBJ√à yo!")
```

#### Kreye obj√®
```python
# Kreye el√®v yo
marie = El√®v("Marie", 20, "3e ane")
jean = El√®v("Jean", 19, "2e ane")

# Ajoute n√≤t yo
marie.ajoute_n√≤t(15)
marie.ajoute_n√≤t(18)
marie.ajoute_n√≤t(20)

jean.ajoute_n√≤t(12)
jean.ajoute_n√≤t(14)
jean.ajoute_n√≤t(16)

# Afiche enf√≤masyon yo
marie.afiche_inf√≤()
jean.afiche_inf√≤()
```

### Konstrikt√® ak Destrikt√®

#### Konstrikt√® `__init__`
```python
class P√®son:
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
        print(f"P√®son {non} kreye")

# Kreye obj√®
p1 = P√®son("Marie", 25)
p2 = P√®son("Jean", 30)
```

#### Destrikt√® `__del__`
```python
class P√®son:
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
        print(f"P√®son {non} kreye")
    
    def __del__(self):
        print(f"P√®son {self.non} detwi")

# Kreye ak detwi obj√®
p1 = P√®son("Marie", 25)
del p1  # Detwi obj√® a
```

### Met√≤d Static ak Instance

#### Met√≤d instance
```python
class Kalkilatris:
    def __init__(self, non):
        self.non = non
        self.istwa = []
    
    def ajoute(self, a, b):
        rezilta = a + b
        self.istwa.append(f"{a} + {b} = {rezilta}")
        return rezilta
    
    def afiche_istwa(self):
        print(f"Istwa {self.non}:")
        for operasyon in self.istwa:
            print(f"  {operasyon}")

# Teste
kalk1 = Kalkilatris("Kalkilatris 1")
kalk2 = Kalkilatris("Kalkilatris 2")

kalk1.ajoute(5, 3)
kalk1.ajoute(10, 7)
kalk2.ajoute(2, 8)

kalk1.afiche_istwa()
kalk2.afiche_istwa()
```

#### Met√≤d static
```python
class Matematik:
    @staticmethod
    def ajoute(a, b):
        return a + b
    
    @staticmethod
    def miltiplike(a, b):
        return a * b
    
    @staticmethod
    def kare(x):
        return x ** 2

# Teste met√≤d static
rezilta1 = Matematik.ajoute(5, 3)
rezilta2 = Matematik.miltiplike(4, 6)
rezilta3 = Matematik.kare(5)

print(f"Ajoute: {rezilta1}")      # 8
print(f"Miltiplike: {rezilta2}")  # 24
print(f"Kare: {rezilta3}")        # 25
```

#### Met√≤d klas
```python
class P√®son:
    kantite_p√®son = 0
    
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
        P√®son.kantite_p√®son += 1
    
    @classmethod
    def kreye_apati_naniv√®rs√®(cls, non, aniv√®rs√®):
        laj = 2024 - aniv√®rs√®
        return cls(non, laj)
    
    @classmethod
    def jwenn_kantite(cls):
        return cls.kantite_p√®son

# Teste
p1 = P√®son("Marie", 25)
p2 = P√®son("Jean", 30)
p3 = P√®son.kreye_apati_naniv√®rs√®("Pierre", 1995)

print(f"Kantite p√®son: {P√®son.jwenn_kantite()}")  # 3
print(f"Laj Pierre: {p3.laj}")  # 29
```

### Eritaj (Inheritance)

#### Eritaj debaz
```python
class Animal:
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
    
    def pale(self):
        print(f"{self.non} ap pale")
    
    def manje(self):
        print(f"{self.non} ap manje")

class Chyen(Animal):
    def __init__(self, non, laj, ras):
        super().__init__(non, laj)
        self.ras = ras
    
    def pale(self):
        print(f"{self.non} ap abw√®")
    
    def kouri(self):
        print(f"{self.non} ap kouri")

# Teste
chen = Chyen("Rex", 3, "Labrador")
chen.pale()    # Rex ap abw√®
chen.manje()   # Rex ap manje
chen.kouri()   # Rex ap kouri
```

#### Eritaj miltipl
```python
class Vol√®:
    def vole(self):
        print("Ap vole nan sy√®l la")

class Naje:
    def naje(self):
        print("Ap naje nan dlo a")

class Kanna(Animal, Vol√®, Naje):
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        super().__init__(non, laj)
    
    def pale(self):
        print(f"{self.non} ap kwaken")

# Teste
kanna = Kanna("Donald", 2)
kanna.pale()   # Donald ap kwaken
kanna.manje()  # Donald ap manje
kanna.vole()   # Ap vole nan sy√®l la
kanna.naje()   # Ap naje nan dlo a
```

#### Met√≤d espesyal
```python
class P√®son:
    def __init__(self, non, laj):
        self.non = non
        self.laj = laj
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"P√®son(non='{self.non}', laj={self.laj})"
    
    def __repr__(self):
        return f"P√®son('{self.non}', {self.laj})"
    
    def __len__(self):
        return len(self.non)
    
    def __add__(self, l√≤t):
        return P√®son(f"{self.non}+{l√≤t.non}", (self.laj + l√≤t.laj) // 2)

# Teste
p1 = P√®son("Marie", 25)
p2 = P√®son("Jean", 30)

print(str(p1))      # P√®son(non='Marie', laj=25)
print(repr(p1))     # P√®son('Marie', 25)
print(len(p1))      # 5
p3 = p1 + p2
print(p3.non)       # Marie+Jean
print(p3.laj)       # 27
```

### Chal√®j: Desine f√≤m yo

#### Klas f√≤m debaz
```python
import math

class F√≤m:
    def __init__(self, non):
        self.non = non
    
    def afiche_nom(self):
        print(f"F√≤m sa a se yon {self.non}")
    
    def kalkile_z√≤n(self):
        pass
    
    def kalkile_perim√®t(self):
        pass

class Rektang(F√≤m):
    def __init__(self, long√®, laj√®):
        super().__init__("rektang")
        self.long√® = long√®
        self.laj√® = laj√®
    
    def kalkile_z√≤n(self):
        return self.long√® * self.laj√®
    
    def kalkile_perim√®t(self):
        return 2 * (self.long√® + self.laj√®)

class S√®k(F√≤m):
    def __init__(self, reyon):
        super().__init__("s√®k")
        self.reyon = reyon
    
    def kalkile_z√≤n(self):
        return math.pi * self.reyon ** 2
    
    def kalkile_perim√®t(self):
        return 2 * math.pi * self.reyon

class Triyang(F√≤m):
    def __init__(self, baz, wot√®, kote1, kote2):
        super().__init__("triyang")
        self.baz = baz
        self.wot√® = wot√®
        self.kote1 = kote1
        self.kote2 = kote2
    
    def kalkile_z√≤n(self):
        return 0.5 * self.baz * self.wot√®
    
    def kalkile_perim√®t(self):
        return self.baz + self.kote1 + self.kote2
```

#### Teste f√≤m yo
```python
# Kreye f√≤m yo
rektang = Rektang(10, 5)
s√®k = S√®k(7)
triyang = Triyang(8, 6, 5, 5)

# Afiche enf√≤masyon yo
f√≤m_yo = [rektang, s√®k, triyang]

for f√≤m in f√≤m_yo:
    f√≤m.afiche_nom()
    print(f"  Z√≤n: {f√≤m.kalkile_z√≤n():.2f}")
    print(f"  Perim√®t: {f√≤m.kalkile_perim√®t():.2f}")
    print()
```

### Egz√®sis Chapit 7

1. **Klas debaz**: Kreye yon klas "Kont" pou jere lajan nan yon kont bank√®
2. **Met√≤d**: Kreye yon klas "Kalkilatris" ak met√≤d static ak instance
3. **Eritaj**: Kreye yon klas "Vehikil" ak klas eritaj "Moto" ak "Machin"
4. **Met√≤d espesyal**: Kreye yon klas "Lis" ak met√≤d espesyal
5. **Chal√®j**: Rezoud pwobl√®m desine f√≤m yo

---

## Chapit 8: Jesyon Er√® ak Eksepsyon (Error Handling and Exceptions) - Eksplikasyon Detaye pou Debitan

### üéØ Objektif Chapit
Apre w fini chapit sa a, w pral kapab:
- **Konprann diferan kalite er√®** - SyntaxError, TypeError, ValueError, ak l√≤t
- **S√®vi ak try/except** - Kaptire ak jere er√® yo
- **Konprann else ak finally** - Bl√≤k adisyon√®l pou jesyon er√®
- **Kreye eksepsyon koutim** - Defini er√® p√®sonalize
- **Devlope yon sist√®m validasyon** - Pwoj√® pratik ak jesyon er√®

> **üí° TIP:** Jesyon er√® se fondasyon pou pwogram solid. Li p√®m√®t ou kreye pwogram ki pa kraze l√® yon bagay ale mal.

### üîß T√®m Kle Pou Chapit Sa A

#### **Er√® Fondamantal**
- **Error** - Pwobl√®m nan k√≤d la
- **Exception** - Er√® ki rive pandan ekzekisyon
- **Try** - Bl√≤k k√≤d pou teste
- **Except** - Bl√≤k pou kaptire er√®
- **Finally** - Bl√≤k ki toujou ekzekite

#### **Kalite Er√®**
- **SyntaxError** - Er√® nan sentaks
- **TypeError** - Er√® nan kalite done
- **ValueError** - Er√® nan val√®
- **NameError** - Varyab pa defini
- **IndexError** - End√®ks pa egziste
- **KeyError** - Kle pa egziste
- **ZeroDivisionError** - Divizyon pa zewo
- **FileNotFoundError** - Fichier pa jwenn

#### **Jesyon Er√®**
- **Raise** - Lanse yon er√®
- **Custom Exception** - Er√® p√®sonalize
- **Exception Hierarchy** - Jerachi er√® yo

---

### üéØ Kisa se "Er√®" (Error) nan Pwogramasyon?

**Definisyon Detaye:**

**Er√®** se pwobl√®m ki rive nan k√≤d la ki anpeche pwogram nan travay k√≤r√®kteman. Li se tankou yon pwobl√®m nan yon rej√®t ki f√® manje a pa bon.

> **üí° TIP:** Pensez a er√® tankou yon pwobl√®m nan yon machin - ou ka jwenn li, konprann li, epi korije li pou machin nan travay ank√≤.

#### üìä Diagram Jesyon Er√®

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[K√≤d N√≤mal] --> B[Er√® Rive]
    B --> C[Try/Except]
    C --> D{Er√® Kaptire?}
    D -->|Wi| E[Jere Er√®]
    D -->|Non| F[Pwogram Kraze]
    E --> G[Kontinye]
    F --> H[Fin]
    G --> I[Kontinye N√≤mal]
```

![Error Handling Visualization](https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1551288049-bebda4e38f71)
*Source: [Unsplash](https://unsplash.com/photos/error) - Photo by [Luca Bravo]*

**Poukisa Er√® Enp√≤tan?**

1. **K√≤r√®ksyon**: Ou ka jwenn ak korije pwobl√®m yo
2. **Stabilite**: Pwogram nan pa kraze l√® yon bagay ale mal
3. **Eksperyans**: Itilizat√® yo genyen yon eksperyans pi bon
4. **Debogaj**: Pi fasil pou jwenn pwobl√®m yo
5. **K√≤d Solid**: Pwogram nan vin pi fiable
6. **Pwodiktivite**: Ou pa p√®di tan ak pwobl√®m yo

---

### üîß Kalite Er√® yo

#### üéØ Kisa se "Diferan Kalite Er√®"?

**Er√®** yo genyen diferan kalite selon kote yo rive ak kisa ki lak√≤z yo. Chak kalite er√® genyen yon siyifikasyon espesifik.

> **üí° TIP:** Er√® yo se tankou diferan kalite maladi - chak genyen yon k√≤z ak yon tretman diferan.

#### üìã Kalite Er√® Enp√≤tan

| Kalite | Deskripsyon | K√≤z | Egzanp |
|--------|-------------|-----|---------|
| **SyntaxError** | Er√® nan sentaks k√≤d | K√≤d mal ekri | `if x = 5:` |
| **TypeError** | Er√® nan kalite done | Kalite pa matche | `"5" + 3` |
| **ValueError** | Er√® nan val√® | Val√® pa bon | `int("abc")` |
| **NameError** | Varyab pa defini | Varyab pa egziste | `print(x)` |
| **IndexError** | End√®ks pa egziste | End√®ks depase limit | `lis[10]` |
| **KeyError** | Kle pa egziste | Kle pa nan diksyon√® | `dik["x"]` |
| **ZeroDivisionError** | Divizyon pa zewo | Divize pa 0 | `5 / 0` |
| **FileNotFoundError** | Fichier pa jwenn | Fichier pa egziste | `open("x.txt")` |

#### üîß Egzanp Detaye Kalite Er√®

**Egzanp 1: SyntaxError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 1: SYNTAXERROR ===")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Oubliye de pwen nan if
# if x = 5:
#     print("Bon")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak == pou konparezon
x = 5
if x == 5:
    print("Bon")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Parant√®z pa f√®men
# print("Bon"

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: F√®men tout parant√®z
print("Bon")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Indentasyon pa bon
# if x == 5:
# print("Bon")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: Indentasyon k√≤r√®k
if x == 5:
    print("Bon")
```

**Egzanp 2: TypeError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 2: TYPEERROR ===")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Pa ka ajoute string ak nimewo
try:
    rezilta = "5" + 3
except TypeError as e:
    print(f"TypeError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: Konv√®ti string nan nimewo
rezilta = int("5") + 3
print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Pa ka miltipliye string ak nimewo
try:
    rezilta = "Hello" * "World"
except TypeError as e:
    print(f"TypeError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: Miltipliye string ak nimewo
rezilta = "Hello" * 3
print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
```

**Egzanp 3: ValueError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 3: VALUERROR ===")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Pa ka konv√®ti string nan nimewo
try:
    nimewo = int("abc")
except ValueError as e:
    print(f"ValueError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak string ki ka konv√®ti
nimewo = int("123")
print(f"Nimewo: {nimewo}")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Pa ka konv√®ti string nan float
try:
    nimewo = float("xyz")
except ValueError as e:
    print(f"ValueError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak string ki ka konv√®ti
nimewo = float("3.14")
print(f"Nimewo: {nimewo}")
```

**Egzanp 4: NameError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 4: NAMEERROR ===")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Varyab pa defini
try:
    print(varyab_pa_defini)
except NameError as e:
    print(f"NameError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: Defini varyab anvan s√®vi ak li
varyab_defini = "Bonjou"
print(f"Varyab: {varyab_defini}")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Fonksyon pa defini
try:
    fonksyon_pa_defini()
except NameError as e:
    print(f"NameError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: Defini fonksyon anvan s√®vi ak li
def fonksyon_defini():
    return "Fonksyon travay"

print(fonksyon_defini())
```

**Egzanp 5: IndexError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 5: INDEXERROR ===")

# Lis ak 5 eleman (end√®ks 0-4)
lis = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]

# ‚ùå Er√®: End√®ks depase limit
try:
    eleman = lis[10]
except IndexError as e:
    print(f"IndexError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak end√®ks ki egziste
eleman = lis[2]
print(f"Eleman nan pozisyon 2: {eleman}")

# ‚ùå Er√®: End√®ks negatif depase limit
try:
    eleman = lis[-10]
except IndexError as e:
    print(f"IndexError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak end√®ks negatif ki egziste
eleman = lis[-1]
print(f"D√®nye eleman: {eleman}")
```

**Egzanp 6: KeyError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 6: KEYERROR ===")

# Diksyon√® ak k√®k kle
dik = {"non": "Marie", "laj": 25, "vil": "P√≤toprens"}

# ‚ùå Er√®: Kle pa egziste
try:
    val√® = dik["telef√≤n"]
except KeyError as e:
    print(f"KeyError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak kle ki egziste
val√® = dik["non"]
print(f"Non: {val√®}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak .get() pou evite KeyError
val√® = dik.get("telef√≤n", "Pa defini")
print(f"Telef√≤n: {val√®}")
```

**Egzanp 7: ZeroDivisionError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 7: ZERODIVISIONERROR ===")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Divize pa zewo
try:
    rezilta = 10 / 0
except ZeroDivisionError as e:
    print(f"ZeroDivisionError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: Tcheke si diviz√® pa zewo
diviz√® = 0
if diviz√® != 0:
    rezilta = 10 / diviz√®
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
else:
    print("Pa ka divize pa zewo")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak try/except
try:
    rezilta = 10 / diviz√®
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("Pa ka divize pa zewo")
```

**Egzanp 8: FileNotFoundError**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 8: FILENOTFOUNDERROR ===")

# ‚ùå Er√®: Fichier pa egziste
try:
    with open("fichier_pa_egziste.txt", "r") as f:
        kontni = f.read()
except FileNotFoundError as e:
    print(f"FileNotFoundError: {e}")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: Tcheke si fichier egziste
import os
non_fichier = "fichier_pa_egziste.txt"
if os.path.exists(non_fichier):
    with open(non_fichier, "r") as f:
        kontni = f.read()
    print(f"Kontni: {kontni}")
else:
    print(f"Fichier {non_fichier} pa egziste")

# ‚úÖ K√≤r√®k: S√®vi ak try/except
try:
    with open(non_fichier, "r") as f:
        kontni = f.read()
    print(f"Kontni: {kontni}")
except FileNotFoundError:
    print(f"Fichier {non_fichier} pa egziste")
```

---

### üîß Try/Except/Else/Finally

#### üéØ Kisa se "Try/Except/Else/Finally"?

**Try/Except/Else/Finally** se estrikti pou jere er√® yo. Yo p√®m√®t ou teste k√≤d, kaptire er√®, epi ekzekite bl√≤k espesifik selon rezilta a.

> **üí° TIP:** Try/Except se tankou yon sekirite - ou ka teste yon bagay, epi si li ale mal, ou ka jere pwobl√®m nan.

#### üìã Sentaks Try/Except/Else/Finally

```python
try:
    # K√≤d pou teste
    k√≤d_pou_teste()
except Er√®Espesifik as e:
    # Jere er√® espesifik
    jere_er√®()
except Er√®L√≤t as e:
    # Jere l√≤t er√®
    jere_l√≤t_er√®()
else:
    # Ekzekite si pa gen er√®
    k√≤d_si_pa_gen_er√®()
finally:
    # Toujou ekzekite
    k√≤d_toujou_ekzekite()
```

#### üîß Egzanp Detaye Try/Except/Else/Finally

**Egzanp 1: Try/Except Debaz**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 1: TRY/EXCEPT DEBAZ ===")

def divize(nimewo1, nimewo2):
    """
    Divize de nimewo
    
    Args:
        nimewo1 (float): Premye nimewo
        nimewo2 (float): Dezy√®m nimewo
    
    Returns:
        float: Rezilta divizyon an
    """
    try:
        rezilta = nimewo1 / nimewo2
        return rezilta
    except ZeroDivisionError:
        print("Er√®: Pa ka divize pa zewo")
        return None
    except TypeError:
        print("Er√®: Param√®t yo dwe nimewo")
        return None

# Teste fonksyon an
print(f"10 / 2 = {divize(10, 2)}")
print(f"10 / 0 = {divize(10, 0)}")
print(f"10 / 'a' = {divize(10, 'a')}")
```

**Egzanp 2: Try/Except ak Plizy√® Er√®**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 2: TRY/EXCEPT AK PLIZY√à ER√à ===")

def kalkile_kare(nimewo):
    """
    Kalkile kare yon nimewo
    
    Args:
        nimewo: Nimewo pou kalkile kare
    
    Returns:
        float: Kare nimewo a
    """
    try:
        # Tcheke si se string
        if isinstance(nimewo, str):
            nimewo = float(nimewo)
        
        # Tcheke si se nimewo
        if not isinstance(nimewo, (int, float)):
            raise TypeError("Param√®t la dwe yon nimewo")
        
        # Kalkile kare
        kare = nimewo ** 2
        return kare
    
    except ValueError as e:
        print(f"ValueError: {e}")
        return None
    except TypeError as e:
        print(f"TypeError: {e}")
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Er√® inatandi: {e}")
        return None

# Teste fonksyon an
print(f"Kare 5 = {kalkile_kare(5)}")
print(f"Kare '3.14' = {kalkile_kare('3.14')}")
print(f"Kare 'abc' = {kalkile_kare('abc')}")
print(f"Kare [1,2,3] = {kalkile_kare([1,2,3])}")
```

**Egzanp 3: Try/Except/Else**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 3: TRY/EXCEPT/ELSE ===")

def li_fichier(non_fichier):
    """
    Li kontni yon fichier
    
    Args:
        non_fichier (str): Non fichier la
    
    Returns:
        str: Kontni fichier la
    """
    try:
        with open(non_fichier, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            kontni = f.read()
    except FileNotFoundError:
        print(f"Fichier {non_fichier} pa jwenn")
        return None
    except PermissionError:
        print(f"Pa gen p√®misyon pou li fichier {non_fichier}")
        return None
    except UnicodeDecodeError:
        print(f"Pa ka dekode fichier {non_fichier}")
        return None
    else:
        print(f"Fichier {non_fichier} li ak siks√®")
        return kontni

# Teste fonksyon an
kontni = li_fichier("fichier_pa_egziste.txt")
if kontni:
    print(f"Kontni: {kontni[:100]}...")
```

**Egzanp 4: Try/Except/Finally**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 4: TRY/EXCEPT/FINALLY ===")

def jere_fichier(non_fichier, kontni):
    """
    Ekri kontni nan yon fichier
    
    Args:
        non_fichier (str): Non fichier la
        kontni (str): Kontni pou ekri
    """
    fichier = None
    try:
        fichier = open(non_fichier, "w", encoding="utf-8")
        fichier.write(kontni)
        print(f"Kontni ekri nan {non_fichier}")
    except PermissionError:
        print(f"Pa gen p√®misyon pou ekri nan {non_fichier}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Er√® inatandi: {e}")
    finally:
        if fichier:
            fichier.close()
            print(f"Fichier {non_fichier} f√®men")

# Teste fonksyon an
jere_fichier("test.txt", "Bonjou nan Python!")
```

**Egzanp 5: Try/Except/Else/Finally Konpl√®**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 5: TRY/EXCEPT/ELSE/FINALLY KONPL√à ===")

def kalkile_mway√®n(lis_nimewo):
    """
    Kalkile mway√®n yon lis nimewo
    
    Args:
        lis_nimewo (list): Lis nimewo yo
    
    Returns:
        float: Mway√®n nimewo yo
    """
    try:
        # Tcheke si lis la vid
        if not lis_nimewo:
            raise ValueError("Lis la vid")
        
        # Tcheke si tout eleman yo se nimewo
        for i, nimewo in enumerate(lis_nimewo):
            if not isinstance(nimewo, (int, float)):
                raise TypeError(f"Eleman nan pozisyon {i} pa se nimewo")
        
        # Kalkile mway√®n
        s√≤m = sum(lis_nimewo)
        mway√®n = s√≤m / len(lis_nimewo)
        
    except ValueError as e:
        print(f"ValueError: {e}")
        return None
    except TypeError as e:
        print(f"TypeError: {e}")
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Er√® inatandi: {e}")
        return None
    else:
        print(f"Kalkil reyisi pou {len(lis_nimewo)} nimewo")
        return mway√®n
    finally:
        print("Kalkil fini")

# Teste fonksyon an
print(f"Mway√®n [1,2,3,4,5]: {kalkile_mway√®n([1,2,3,4,5])}")
print(f"Mway√®n []: {kalkile_mway√®n([])}")
print(f"Mway√®n [1,'a',3]: {kalkile_mway√®n([1,'a',3])}")
```

---

### üîß Eksepsyon Koutim

#### üéØ Kisa se "Eksepsyon Koutim"?

**Eksepsyon Koutim** se er√® p√®sonalize ke ou kreye pou sitiyasyon espesifik nan pwogram ou an. Yo p√®m√®t ou kreye er√® ki genyen siyifikasyon espesifik pou aplikasyon ou an.

> **üí° TIP:** Eksepsyon koutim se tankou yon mesaj er√® p√®sonalize - ou ka kreye mesaj ki espesifik pou pwogram ou an.

#### üìã Sentaks Eksepsyon Koutim

```python
class NonEksepsyon(Exception):
    """
    Eksepsyon koutim
    """
    def __init__(self, mesaj):
        self.mesaj = mesaj
        super().__init__(self.mesaj)

# S√®vi ak eksepsyon koutim
raise NonEksepsyon("Mesaj er√®")
```

#### üîß Egzanp Detaye Eksepsyon Koutim

**Egzanp 1: Eksepsyon Koutim Debaz**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 1: EKSEPSYON KOUTIM DEBAZ ===")

class Er√®Laj(Exception):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou laj ki pa valab
    """
    def __init__(self, laj):
        self.laj = laj
        super().__init__(f"Laj {laj} pa valab. Laj la dwe ant 0 ak 150")

class Er√®Non(Exception):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou non ki pa valab
    """
    def __init__(self, non):
        self.non = non
        super().__init__(f"Non '{non}' pa valab. Non la dwe genyen omwen 2 karakt√®")

def valide_p√®son(non, laj):
    """
    Valide enf√≤masyon p√®son
    
    Args:
        non (str): Non p√®son nan
        laj (int): Laj p√®son nan
    """
    # Valide non
    if not non or len(non) < 2:
        raise Er√®Non(non)
    
    # Valide laj
    if not isinstance(laj, int) or laj < 0 or laj > 150:
        raise Er√®Laj(laj)
    
    print(f"Enf√≤masyon valide: {non}, {laj} ane")

# Teste fonksyon an
try:
    valide_p√®son("Marie", 25)
except Er√®Non as e:
    print(f"Er√® Non: {e}")
except Er√®Laj as e:
    print(f"Er√® Laj: {e}")

try:
    valide_p√®son("A", 25)
except Er√®Non as e:
    print(f"Er√® Non: {e}")
except Er√®Laj as e:
    print(f"Er√® Laj: {e}")

try:
    valide_p√®son("Marie", -5)
except Er√®Non as e:
    print(f"Er√® Non: {e}")
except Er√®Laj as e:
    print(f"Er√® Laj: {e}")
```

**Egzanp 2: Eksepsyon Koutim Konpl√®ks**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 2: EKSEPSYON KOUTIM KONPL√àKS ===")

class Er√®KontBank√®(Exception):
    """
    Eksepsyon debaz pou kont bank√®
    """
    pass

class Er√®BalansEnsuisan(Er√®KontBank√®):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou balans ensuisan
    """
    def __init__(self, balans, kantite):
        self.balans = balans
        self.kantite = kantite
        super().__init__(f"Balans ensuisan: ${balans:.2f}, Bezwen: ${kantite:.2f}")

class Er√®KantiteNegatif(Er√®KontBank√®):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou kantite negatif
    """
    def __init__(self, kantite):
        self.kantite = kantite
        super().__init__(f"Kantite negatif pa p√®m√®t: ${kantite:.2f}")

class Er√®KantiteTw√≤Gwo(Er√®KontBank√®):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou kantite tw√≤ gwo
    """
    def __init__(self, kantite, limit):
        self.kantite = kantite
        self.limit = limit
        super().__init__(f"Kantite tw√≤ gwo: ${kantite:.2f}, Limit: ${limit:.2f}")

class KontBank√®:
    """
    Klas pou kont bank√®
    """
    
    def __init__(self, non, balans_initial=0, limit_retire=1000):
        self.non = non
        self.balans = balans_initial
        self.limit_retire = limit_retire
        print(f"Kont kreye pou {self.non} ak balans ${self.balans:.2f}")
    
    def depoze(self, kantite):
        """
        Depoze lajan nan kont la
        
        Args:
            kantite (float): Kantite lajan pou depoze
        """
        if kantite < 0:
            raise Er√®KantiteNegatif(kantite)
        
        self.balans += kantite
        print(f"${kantite:.2f} depoze. Nouvo balans: ${self.balans:.2f}")
    
    def retire(self, kantite):
        """
        Retire lajan nan kont la
        
        Args:
            kantite (float): Kantite lajan pou retire
        """
        if kantite < 0:
            raise Er√®KantiteNegatif(kantite)
        
        if kantite > self.limit_retire:
            raise Er√®KantiteTw√≤Gwo(kantite, self.limit_retire)
        
        if kantite > self.balans:
            raise Er√®BalansEnsuisan(self.balans, kantite)
        
        self.balans -= kantite
        print(f"${kantite:.2f} retire. Nouvo balans: ${self.balans:.2f}")

# Teste kont bank√®
kont = KontBank√®("Marie", 1000, 500)

try:
    kont.depoze(200)
except Er√®KontBank√® as e:
    print(f"Er√® Kont: {e}")

try:
    kont.retire(300)
except Er√®KontBank√® as e:
    print(f"Er√® Kont: {e}")

try:
    kont.retire(600)
except Er√®KontBank√® as e:
    print(f"Er√® Kont: {e}")

try:
    kont.retire(-100)
except Er√®KontBank√® as e:
    print(f"Er√® Kont: {e}")
```

**Egzanp 3: Eksepsyon ak Jerachi**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 3: EKSEPSYON AK JERACHI ===")

class Er√®Validasyon(Exception):
    """
    Eksepsyon debaz pou validasyon
    """
    pass

class Er√®F√≤ma(Er√®Validasyon):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou f√≤ma ki pa bon
    """
    pass

class Er√®Email(Er√®F√≤ma):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou email ki pa valab
    """
    def __init__(self, email):
        self.email = email
        super().__init__(f"Email '{email}' pa valab")

class Er√®Telef√≤n(Er√®F√≤ma):
    """
    Eksepsyon pou telef√≤n ki pa valab
    """
    def __init__(self, telef√≤n):
        self.telef√≤n = telef√≤n
        super().__init__(f"Telef√≤n '{telef√≤n}' pa valab")

def valide_email(email):
    """
    Valide adr√®s email
    
    Args:
        email (str): Adr√®s email la
    """
    if "@" not in email or "." not in email:
        raise Er√®Email(email)
    
    print(f"Email '{email}' valide")

def valide_telef√≤n(telef√≤n):
    """
    Valide nimewo telef√≤n
    
    Args:
        telef√≤n (str): Nimewo telef√≤n la
    """
    # Tcheke si se jis chif
    if not telef√≤n.isdigit():
        raise Er√®Telef√≤n(telef√≤n)
    
    # Tcheke long√®
    if len(telef√≤n) != 10:
        raise Er√®Telef√≤n(telef√≤n)
    
    print(f"Telef√≤n '{telef√≤n}' valide")

# Teste validasyon
try:
    valide_email("marie@example.com")
except Er√®Validasyon as e:
    print(f"Er√® Validasyon: {e}")

try:
    valide_email("email_pa_valab")
except Er√®Validasyon as e:
    print(f"Er√® Validasyon: {e}")

try:
    valide_telef√≤n("1234567890")
except Er√®Validasyon as e:
    print(f"Er√® Validasyon: {e}")

try:
    valide_telef√≤n("123abc")
except Er√®Validasyon as e:
    print(f"Er√® Validasyon: {e}")
```

---

### üìä Resime Jesyon Er√®

#### üéØ T√®m Enp√≤tan yo

| T√®m | Deskripsyon | Egzanp |
|-----|-------------|---------|
| **Error** | Pwobl√®m nan k√≤d la | `SyntaxError` |
| **Exception** | Er√® ki rive pandan ekzekisyon | `TypeError` |
| **Try** | Bl√≤k k√≤d pou teste | `try:` |
| **Except** | Bl√≤k pou kaptire er√® | `except TypeError:` |
| **Else** | Bl√≤k si pa gen er√® | `else:` |
| **Finally** | Bl√≤k ki toujou ekzekite | `finally:` |
| **Raise** | Lanse yon er√® | `raise ValueError()` |
| **Custom Exception** | Er√® p√®sonalize | `class Er√®Koutim(Exception)` |

#### üîß R√®g Enp√≤tan

1. **Try/Except**: Toujou s√®vi ak try/except pou k√≤d ki ka ale mal
2. **Specific Exceptions**: Kaptire er√® espesifik anvan er√® jeneral
3. **Custom Exceptions**: Kreye er√® p√®sonalize pou sitiyasyon espesifik
4. **Finally**: S√®vi ak finally pou netwayaj
5. **Error Messages**: Ekri mesaj er√® ki kl√® ak itil

#### ‚ö†Ô∏è Er√® Komen

1. **Pa s√®vi ak try/except** pou k√≤d ki ka ale mal
2. **Kaptire er√® jeneral** anvan er√® espesifik
3. **Pa ekri mesaj er√®** ki pa kl√®
4. **Oubliye finally** pou netwayaj
5. **Pa teste k√≤d** ak diferan kalite er√®

---

### üéÆ Egz√®sis Pratik

**Egz√®sis 1: Kalkilatris ak Jesyon Er√®**
Kreye yon kalkilatris ki jere tout kalite er√®.

**Egz√®sis 2: Sist√®m Validasyon**
Kreye yon sist√®m validasyon ak eksepsyon koutim.

**Egz√®sis 3: Gestion√® Fichier**
Kreye yon gestion√® fichier ki jere er√® yo.

**Egz√®sis 4: Jw√®t ak Jesyon Er√®**
Kreye yon jw√®t ki jere er√® yo gracieusement.
2. **Sekirite**: Pwogram nan pa kraze
3. **Eksperyans**: Itilizat√® a pa jwenn mesaj konfizyon
4. **Devlopman**: Ou ka aprann nan er√® yo
5. **Pwofesyon√®l**: K√≤d la pi solid ak fiable

**Analoji ki fasil konprann:**
- **Er√®** = Tankou yon pwobl√®m nan yon rej√®t
- **Try/Except** = Tankou yon plan B pou rej√®t la
- **Exception** = Tankou yon pwobl√®m espesifik
- **Debugging** = Tankou jwenn ak korije pwobl√®m nan rej√®t la

### üîß T√®m Fondamantal nan Jesyon Er√®

#### 1. **Error** (Er√®) - Pwobl√®m Nan K√≤d

**Kisa se "Error"?**

**Error** se yon pwobl√®m nan k√≤d la ki anpeche pwogram nan travay. Li se tankou yon er√® nan yon rej√®t ki f√® manje a pa bon.

**Poukisa Error Enp√≤tan?**
- Li montre ou kote pwobl√®m nan ye
- Li ede ou aprann nan er√® yo
- Li p√®m√®t ou korije k√≤d la

**Kalite Er√®:**
- **Syntax Error** - K√≤d la pa swiv r√®g yo
- **Runtime Error** - Pwobl√®m pandan kouri pwogram nan
- **Logic Error** - K√≤d la travay men pa f√® sa ou vle

#### 2. **Exception** (Eksepsyon) - Er√® Espesifik

**Kisa se "Exception"?**

**Exception** se yon kalite er√® espesifik ki rive pandan kouri pwogram nan. Li se tankou yon pwobl√®m espesifik nan yon rej√®t.

**Poukisa Exception Enp√≤tan?**
- Yo bay enf√≤masyon detaye sou pwobl√®m nan
- Ou ka atrape yo ak try/except
- Yo ede ou jere pwobl√®m yo

**Egzanp Exception:**
```python
# ValueError - Val√® pa bon
try:
    nimewo = int("abc")  # Sa va bay ValueError
except ValueError:
    print("Val√® a pa bon!")

# ZeroDivisionError - Divize pa zewo
try:
    rezilta = 10 / 0  # Sa va bay ZeroDivisionError
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("Ou pa ka divize pa zewo!")
```

#### 3. **try** - Eseye K√≤d

**Kisa se "try"?**

**try** se yon mo kle nan Python ki di "Eseye k√≤d sa a, men si gen pwobl√®m, f√® sa l√≤t bagay". Li se tankou di "Eseye f√® rej√®t sa a, men si li pa bon, f√® yon l√≤t bagay".

**Poukisa try Enp√≤tan?**
- Li p√®m√®t ou eseye k√≤d ki ka gen pwobl√®m
- Li anpeche pwogram nan kraze
- Li bay ou kontw√≤l sou er√® yo

**Egzanp try:**
```python
try:
    # K√≤d ki ka gen pwobl√®m
    nimewo = int(input("Antre yon nimewo: "))
    rezilta = 10 / nimewo
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
except:
    # Sa pou f√® si gen pwobl√®m
    print("Yon pwobl√®m rive!")
```

#### 4. **except** - Jere Er√®

**Kisa se "except"?**

**except** se yon mo kle nan Python ki di "Si gen er√®, f√® sa". Li se tankou di "Si rej√®t la pa bon, f√® sa l√≤t bagay".

**Poukisa except Enp√≤tan?**
- Li jere er√® yo
- Li anpeche pwogram nan kraze
- Li bay mesaj itil pou itilizat√® a

**Egzanp except:**
```python
try:
    nimewo = int(input("Antre yon nimewo: "))
    rezilta = 10 / nimewo
except ValueError:
    print("Ou pa antre yon nimewo valab!")
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("Ou pa ka divize pa zewo!")
except Exception as e:
    print(f"Yon er√® rive: {e}")
```

#### 5. **finally** - Toujou F√®

**Kisa se "finally"?**

**finally** se yon mo kle nan Python ki di "Toujou f√® sa, menm si gen er√® oswa pa". Li se tankou di "Toujou lave asy√®t yo, menm si manje a pa bon".

**Poukisa finally Enp√≤tan?**
- Li asire ke k√®k bagay toujou f√®t
- Li netwaye resous yo
- Li f√®men fichier yo

**Egzanp finally:**
```python
try:
    fichier = open("done.txt", "r")
    kontni = fichier.read()
except FileNotFoundError:
    print("Fichier a pa jwenn!")
finally:
    fichier.close()  # Toujou f√®men fichier la
```

#### 6. **else** - Si Pa Gen Er√®

**Kisa se "else" nan try/except?**

**else** nan try/except se yon mo kle ki di "Si pa gen er√®, f√® sa". Li se tankou di "Si rej√®t la bon, f√® sa".

**Poukisa else Enp√≤tan?**
- Li f√® aksyon si tout bagay bon
- Li separe k√≤d ki gen pwobl√®m ak k√≤d ki bon
- Li f√® k√≤d la pi kl√®

**Egzanp else:**
```python
try:
    nimewo = int(input("Antre yon nimewo: "))
    rezilta = 10 / nimewo
except ValueError:
    print("Ou pa antre yon nimewo valab!")
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("Ou pa ka divize pa zewo!")
else:
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")  # F√® si pa gen er√®
```

### üîß Kalite Er√® Yo

#### 1. **SyntaxError** - Er√® Nan R√®g

**Kisa se "SyntaxError"?**

**SyntaxError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® k√≤d la pa swiv r√®g Python yo. Li se tankou yon er√® gram√® nan yon fraz.

**Egzanp SyntaxError:**
```python
# ‚ùå SYNTAX ERROR
print("Hello world"  # Manke parant√®z )

# ‚ùå SYNTAX ERROR
if laj >= 18  # Manke kol√≤n (:)
    print("Ou maj√®")

# ‚úÖ SYNTAX K√íR√àK
print("Hello world")
if laj >= 18:
    print("Ou maj√®")
```

#### 2. **NameError** - Non Pa Defini

**Kisa se "NameError"?**

**NameError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® ou s√®vi ak yon non ki pa defini. Li se tankou s√®vi ak yon mo ki pa nan diksyon√® a.

**Egzanp NameError:**
```python
# ‚ùå NAME ERROR
print(nome_varyab)  # nome_varyab pa defini

# ‚úÖ K√íR√àK
nome_varyab = "Bonjou"
print(nome_varyab)
```

#### 3. **TypeError** - Kalite Done Pa Bon

**Kisa se "TypeError"?**

**TypeError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® ou s√®vi ak kalite done ki pa konpatib. Li se tankou eseye ajoute p√≤m ak z√≤r√®j.

**Egzanp TypeError:**
```python
# ‚ùå TYPE ERROR
print("5" + 3)  # Pa ka ajoute string ak nimewo

# ‚úÖ K√íR√àK
print("5" + str(3))  # Konv√®ti nimewo a nan string
print(5 + 3)         # Ajoute de nimewo
```

#### 4. **ValueError** - Val√® Pa Valab

**Kisa se "ValueError"?**

**ValueError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® val√® a pa bon pou operasyon an. Li se tankou eseye mete yon kaw√≤t nan yon f√≤mil pou gato.

**Egzanp ValueError:**
```python
# ‚ùå VALUE ERROR
int("abc")  # Pa ka konv√®ti "abc" nan nimewo

# ‚úÖ K√íR√àK
int("123")  # Konv√®ti "123" nan nimewo 123
```

#### 5. **IndexError** - Endeks Pa Egziste

**Kisa se "IndexError"?**

**IndexError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® ou eseye aksede yon pozisyon ki pa egziste nan yon lis. Li se tankou eseye jwenn eleman 10 nan yon lis ki gen s√®lman 5 eleman.

**Egzanp IndexError:**
```python
# ‚ùå INDEX ERROR
lis = [1, 2, 3]
print(lis[5])  # Endeks 5 pa egziste

# ‚úÖ K√íR√àK
lis = [1, 2, 3]
print(lis[2])  # Endeks 2 egziste
```

#### 6. **KeyError** - Kle Pa Egziste

**Kisa se "KeyError"?**

**KeyError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® ou eseye aksede yon kle ki pa egziste nan yon diksyone. Li se tankou eseye jwenn yon mo ki pa nan diksyon√® a.

**Egzanp KeyError:**
```python
# ‚ùå KEY ERROR
dik = {"a": 1, "b": 2}
print(dik["c"])  # Kle "c" pa egziste

# ‚úÖ K√íR√àK
dik = {"a": 1, "b": 2}
print(dik["a"])  # Kle "a" egziste
```

#### 7. **ZeroDivisionError** - Divize Pa Zewo

**Kisa se "ZeroDivisionError"?**

**ZeroDivisionError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® ou eseye divize pa zewo. Li se tankou eseye pataje yon bagay ant zewo moun.

**Egzanp ZeroDivisionError:**
```python
# ‚ùå ZERO DIVISION ERROR
rezilta = 10 / 0

# ‚úÖ K√íR√àK
try:
    rezilta = 10 / 0
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("Ou pa ka divize pa zewo!")
```

#### 8. **FileNotFoundError** - Fichier Pa Jwenn

**Kisa se "FileNotFoundError"?**

**FileNotFoundError** se yon er√® ki rive l√® ou eseye ouvri yon fichier ki pa egziste. Li se tankou eseye ouvri yon liv ki pa nan bibliyot√®k la.

**Egzanp FileNotFoundError:**
```python
# ‚ùå FILE NOT FOUND ERROR
fichier = open("fichier_ki_pa_egziste.txt", "r")

# ‚úÖ K√íR√àK
try:
    fichier = open("done.txt", "r")
    kontni = fichier.read()
except FileNotFoundError:
    print("Fichier a pa jwenn!")
```

### üéÆ Egzanp Pratik Konpl√®

```python
# üéÆ EGZANP AMIZAN: Ou nan yon restoran ak chef

print("üçΩÔ∏è SITUASYON: Ou nan yon restoran ak chef")
print("=" * 45)

# 1. TRY/EXCEPT DEBAZ
print("1Ô∏è‚É£ TRY/EXCEPT DEBAZ")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'Eseye f√® rej√®t la, men si li pa bon, f√® sa l√≤t bagay'")

def divize_pri(pri_total, kantite_moun):
    """Divize pri total ant kantite moun"""
    try:
        pri_pa_moun = pri_total / kantite_moun
        print(f"   üí∞ Chak moun peye: {pri_pa_moun:.2f} goud")
        return pri_pa_moun
    except ZeroDivisionError:
        print("   ‚ùå Ou pa ka divize ant 0 moun!")
        return 0
    except TypeError:
        print("   ‚ùå Ou dwe antre nimewo!")
        return 0

# Teste divize_pri
divize_pri(100, 4)    # K√≤r√®k
divize_pri(100, 0)    # ZeroDivisionError
divize_pri("100", 4)  # TypeError

print()

# 2. TRY/EXCEPT/ELSE
print("2Ô∏è‚É£ TRY/EXCEPT/ELSE")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'Eseye f√® rej√®t la, si li pa bon f√® sa l√≤t bagay, si li bon f√® sa'")

def kalkile_tip(pri, pousantaj):
    """Kalkile tip pou pri a"""
    try:
        tip = pri * (pousantaj / 100)
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        print("   ‚ùå Ou dwe antre nimewo valab!")
        tip = 0
    except ZeroDivisionError:
        print("   ‚ùå Pousantaj la pa ka zewo!")
        tip = 0
    else:
        print(f"   ‚úÖ Tip kalkile: {tip:.2f} goud")
        print(f"   üí≥ Total: {pri + tip:.2f} goud")
    finally:
        print("   üßπ Netwaye kalkil yo...")

# Teste kalkile_tip
kalkile_tip(100, 15)     # K√≤r√®k
kalkile_tip("100", 15)   # TypeError
kalkile_tip(100, "15")   # TypeError

print()

# 3. TRY/EXCEPT/FINALLY
print("3Ô∏è‚É£ TRY/EXCEPT/FINALLY")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'Eseye f√® rej√®t la, menm si li pa bon, toujou lave asy√®t yo'")

def li_fichier_rej√®t(nom_fichier):
    """Li fichier rej√®t la"""
    fichier = None
    try:
        fichier = open(nom_fichier, "r")
        kontni = fichier.read()
        print(f"   üìñ Rej√®t la: {kontni}")
        return kontni
    except FileNotFoundError:
        print(f"   ‚ùå Fichier {nom_fichier} pa jwenn!")
        return ""
    except PermissionError:
        print(f"   ‚ùå Ou pa gen p√®misyon pou li {nom_fichier}!")
        return ""
    finally:
        if fichier:
            fichier.close()
            print("   üîí Fichier la f√®men")

# Teste li_fichier_rej√®t
li_fichier_rej√®t("rej√®t.txt")        # Si fichier la egziste
li_fichier_rej√®t("pa_egziste.txt")   # Si fichier la pa egziste

print()

# 4. JERE PLIZY√à ER√à
print("4Ô∏è‚É£ JERE PLIZY√à ER√à")
print("   üí° Pensez: 'Eseye f√® rej√®t la, men jere diferan kalite pwobl√®m'")

def kalkile_pri_manje(pri, kantite, tip):
    """Kalkile pri manje ak tip"""
    try:
        # Konv√®ti string yo nan nimewo
        pri = float(pri)
        kantite = int(kantite)
        tip = float(tip)
        
        # Kalkile pri total
        pri_total = pri * kantite
        tip_montan = pri_total * (tip / 100)
        total = pri_total + tip_montan
        
        print(f"   üí∞ Pri yon s√®l: {pri} goud")
        print(f"   üìä Kantite: {kantite}")
        print(f"   üí≥ Pri total: {pri_total} goud")
        print(f"   üéÅ Tip ({tip}%): {tip_montan:.2f} goud")
        print(f"   üí∏ Total final: {total:.2f} goud")
        
        return total
        
    except ValueError as e:
        print(f"   ‚ùå Val√® pa bon: {e}")
        print("   üí° Asire w ke ou antre nimewo!")
        return 0
    except ZeroDivisionError:
        print("   ‚ùå Ou pa ka divize pa zewo!")
        return 0
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ‚ùå Yon er√® inatandi rive: {e}")
        return 0

# Teste kalkile_pri_manje
kalkile_pri_manje("25.50", "3", "15")    # K√≤r√®k
kalkile_pri_manje("abc", "3", "15")      # ValueError
kalkile_pri_manje("25.50", "0", "15")    # ZeroDivisionError

print()

print("üéâ BRAVO! Ou konprann JESYON ER√à ak EKSEPSYON yo!")
```

### Try ak Except

#### Try/Except debaz
```python
try:
    nimewo = int(input("Antre yon nimewo: "))
    rezilta = 10 / nimewo
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
except ValueError:
    print("Ou pa antre yon nimewo valab!")
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("Ou pa ka divize pa zewo!")
except Exception as e:
    print(f"Yon er√® rive: {e}")
```

#### Try/Except/Else
```python
try:
    nimewo = int(input("Antre yon nimewo: "))
    rezilta = 10 / nimewo
except ValueError:
    print("Ou pa antre yon nimewo valab!")
except ZeroDivisionError:
    print("Ou pa ka divize pa zewo!")
else:
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
    print("Operasyon an reyisi!")
```

#### Try/Except/Finally
```python
try:
    fichier = open("test.txt", "r")
    kontni = fichier.read()
    print(kontni)
except FileNotFoundError:
    print("Fichier a pa egziste!")
except Exception as e:
    print(f"Yon er√® rive: {e}")
finally:
    print("Nou toujou ekzekite sa a")
    # Fichier yo toujou f√®men nan finally
```

### Eksepsyon Koutim

#### Kreye eksepsyon koutim
```python
class Er√®Laj(Exception):
    """Eksepsyon pou laj ki pa valab"""
    def __init__(self, laj, mesaj="Laj pa valab"):
        self.laj = laj
        self.mesaj = mesaj
        super().__init__(self.mesaj)

class Er√®N√≤t(Exception):
    """Eksepsyon pou n√≤t ki pa valab"""
    def __init__(self, n√≤t, mesaj="N√≤t pa valab"):
        self.n√≤t = n√≤t
        self.mesaj = mesaj
        super().__init__(self.mesaj)
```

#### S√®vi ak eksepsyon koutim
```python
def kreye_el√®v(non, laj, n√≤t):
    # Teste laj
    if laj < 0 or laj > 120:
        raise Er√®Laj(laj, f"Laj {laj} pa valab. Laj dwe ant 0 ak 120")
    
    # Teste n√≤t
    if n√≤t < 0 or n√≤t > 20:
        raise Er√®N√≤t(n√≤t, f"N√≤t {n√≤t} pa valab. N√≤t dwe ant 0 ak 20")
    
    return {"non": non, "laj": laj, "n√≤t": n√≤t}

# Teste
try:
    el√®v1 = kreye_el√®v("Marie", 25, 15)
    print("El√®v kreye:", el√®v1)
    
    el√®v2 = kreye_el√®v("Jean", 150, 18)  # Er√® laj
except Er√®Laj as e:
    print(f"Er√® laj: {e}")
except Er√®N√≤t as e:
    print(f"Er√® n√≤t: {e}")
```

### Chal√®j: Argumant ki pa bon

#### Pwobl√®m: Fonksyon ak argumant ki pa valab
```python
def kalkile_mway√®n(n√≤t_yo):
    """Kalkile mway√®n n√≤t yo"""
    if not n√≤t_yo:
        raise ValueError("Lis n√≤t yo pa ka vid")
    
    for n√≤t in n√≤t_yo:
        if not isinstance(n√≤t, (int, float)):
            raise TypeError(f"N√≤t '{n√≤t}' pa se yon nimewo")
        if n√≤t < 0 or n√≤t > 20:
            raise ValueError(f"N√≤t {n√≤t} pa valab. Dwe ant 0 ak 20")
    
    return sum(n√≤t_yo) / len(n√≤t_yo)

# Teste
test_kas_yo = [
    [15, 18, 20],           # Normal
    [],                     # Lis vid
    [15, "18", 20],         # N√≤t pa nimewo
    [15, 25, 20],           # N√≤t ki pi gran pase 20
    [15, -5, 20],           # N√≤t negatif
]

for n√≤t_yo in test_kas_yo:
    try:
        mway√®n = kalkile_mway√®n(n√≤t_yo)
        print(f"N√≤t yo: {n√≤t_yo} ‚Üí Mway√®n: {mway√®n:.2f}")
    except ValueError as e:
        print(f"N√≤t yo: {n√≤t_yo} ‚Üí Er√® val√®: {e}")
    except TypeError as e:
        print(f"N√≤t yo: {n√≤t_yo} ‚Üí Er√® kalite: {e}")
```

### Egz√®sis Chapit 8

1. **Try/Except**: Kreye yon pwogram ki li yon fichier ak jesyon er√®
2. **Eksepsyon koutim**: Kreye yon klas eksepsyon pou valide enf√≤masyon el√®v
3. **Finally**: Kreye yon pwogram ki s√®vi ak finally pou f√®men resous
4. **Chal√®j**: Rezoud pwobl√®m argumant ki pa bon la

---

## Chapit 9: Threads ak Pwosesis (Multithreading and Multiprocessing) - Eksplikasyon Detaye pou Debitan

### üéØ Objektif Chapit
Apre w fini chapit sa a, w pral kapab:
- **Konprann diferans threads ak pwosesis** - Kisa yo ye ak poukisa yo enp√≤tan
- **S√®vi ak multithreading** - F√® plizy√® travay an menm tan nan yon pwogram
- **Konprann synchronization** - Evite konfli l√® plizy√® threads travay ansanm
- **S√®vi ak multiprocessing** - S√®vi ak plizy√® pwosesis pou travay pi vit
- **Devlope yon sist√®m monit√≤** - Pwoj√® pratik ak paralelizasyon

> **üí° TIP:** Threads ak pwosesis se fason pi efikas pou f√® travay ki pran tan. Yo p√®m√®t ou s√®vi ak tout kapasite konpit√® a.

### üîß T√®m Kle Pou Chapit Sa A

#### **Threads Fondamantal**
- **Thread** - Yon fil ekzekisyon nan yon pwogram
- **Multithreading** - Plizy√® threads travay ansanm
- **Synchronization** - Kontw√≤l aks√® nan resous partaje
- **Lock** - Mekanik pou evite konfli
- **Queue** - Kanal pou kominikasyon ant threads

#### **Pwosesis Fondamantal**
- **Process** - Yon pwogram ki kouri endependan
- **Multiprocessing** - Plizy√® pwosesis travay ansanm
- **Pool** - Gwoup pwosesis pou travay
- **Pipe** - Kanal pou kominikasyon ant pwosesis
- **Manager** - Jere done partaje ant pwosesis

#### **Konsep Avanse**
- **Concurrency** - F√® plizy√® bagay an menm tan
- **Parallelism** - F√® plizy√® bagay vreman an menm tan
- **Race Condition** - Konfli l√® plizy√® threads aksede menm done
- **Deadlock** - Threads yo bloke youn l√≤t
- **GIL** - Global Interpreter Lock nan Python

---

### üéØ Kisa se "Threads ak Pwosesis"?

**Definisyon Detaye:**

**Threads ak Pwosesis** se teknik Python yo ki p√®m√®t pwogram nan f√® plizy√® bagay an menm tan. Li se tankou gen plizy√® moun ki travay sou menm pwoj√® a nan menm tan.

> **üí° TIP:** Pensez a threads tankou plizy√® moun ki travay nan menm ofis la, epi pwosesis tankou plizy√® ofis ki travay sou menm pwoj√® a.

#### üìä Diagram Threads vs Pwosesis

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Pwogram Prensipal] --> B[Thread 1]
    A --> C[Thread 2]
    A --> D[Thread 3]
    B --> E[Travay 1]
    C --> F[Travay 2]
    D --> G[Travay 3]
    
    H[Pwosesis 1] --> I[Travay 1]
    J[Pwosesis 2] --> K[Travay 2]
    L[Pwosesis 3] --> M[Travay 3]
    
    style A fill:#e1f5fe
    style H fill:#f3e5f5
    style J fill:#f3e5f5
    style L fill:#f3e5f5
```

![Threads and Processes Visualization](https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1551288049-bebda4e38f71)
*Source: [Unsplash](https://unsplash.com/photos/parallel) - Photo by [Luca Bravo]*

**Poukisa Threads ak Pwosesis Enp√≤tan?**

1. **Vit√®s**: F√® travay yo pi vit
2. **Efikasite**: S√®vi ak tout kapasite konpit√® a
3. **Repons**: Pwogram nan reponn pi vit
4. **Scalabilit√©**: Kapab jere plis travay
5. **Eksperyans**: Itilizat√® yo pa tann
6. **Pwodiktivite**: F√® plis nan mwens tan

---

### üîß Diferans Threads vs Pwosesis

#### üéØ Kisa se "Diferans Threads ak Pwosesis"?

**Threads** se fil ekzekisyon nan yon menm pwogram ki pataje memwa.
**Pwosesis** se pwogram endependan ki genyen memwa pa yo.

> **üí° TIP:** Threads se tankou plizy√® moun ki travay nan menm chanm la, pwosesis se tankou plizy√® moun ki travay nan chanm diferan.

#### üìã Konparezon Threads vs Pwosesis

| Karakteristik | Threads | Pwosesis |
|---------------|---------|----------|
| **Memwa** | Pataje | Endependan |
| **Kominikasyon** | Fasil | Pi difisil |
| **Kreasyon** | Pi vit | Pi dousman |
| **Sekirite** | Pi p√® | Pi sekirize |
| **GIL** | Afekte | Pa afekte |
| **I/O** | Bon | Bon |
| **CPU** | Limite | Pi bon |

#### üîß Egzanp Detaye Diferans

**Egzanp 1: Threads Debaz**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 1: THREADS DEBAZ ===")

import threading
import time

def travay_thread(non, kantite):
    """
    Fonksyon pou travay nan thread
    
    Args:
        non (str): Non thread la
        kantite (int): Kantite travay pou f√®
    """
    print(f"Thread {non} k√≤manse")
    for i in range(kantite):
        print(f"Thread {non}: Travay {i+1}")
        time.sleep(0.1)  # Simule travay ki pran tan
    print(f"Thread {non} fini")

# Kreye threads
thread1 = threading.Thread(target=travay_thread, args=("A", 5))
thread2 = threading.Thread(target=travay_thread, args=("B", 3))

# K√≤manse threads
print("K√≤manse threads...")
thread1.start()
thread2.start()

# Tann threads yo fini
thread1.join()
thread2.join()

print("Tout threads fini!")
```

**Egzanp 2: Pwosesis Debaz**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 2: PWOSESIS DEBAZ ===")

import multiprocessing
import time

def travay_pwosesis(non, kantite):
    """
    Fonksyon pou travay nan pwosesis
    
    Args:
        non (str): Non pwosesis la
        kantite (int): Kantite travay pou f√®
    """
    print(f"Pwosesis {non} k√≤manse")
    for i in range(kantite):
        print(f"Pwosesis {non}: Travay {i+1}")
        time.sleep(0.1)  # Simule travay ki pran tan
    print(f"Pwosesis {non} fini")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Kreye pwosesis yo
    pwosesis1 = multiprocessing.Process(target=travay_pwosesis, args=("X", 5))
    pwosesis2 = multiprocessing.Process(target=travay_pwosesis, args=("Y", 3))

    # K√≤manse pwosesis yo
    print("K√≤manse pwosesis...")
    pwosesis1.start()
    pwosesis2.start()

    # Tann pwosesis yo fini
    pwosesis1.join()
    pwosesis2.join()

    print("Tout pwosesis fini!")
```

**Egzanp 3: Konparezon Vit√®s**

```python
print("=== EGZANP 3: KONPAREZON VIT√àS ===")

import threading
import multiprocessing
import time

def kalkile_kare(nimewo):
    """
    Kalkile kare yon nimewo (travay ki pran tan)
    
    Args:
        nimewo (int): Nimewo pou kalkile kare
    
    Returns:
        int: Kare nimewo a
    """
    # Simule travay ki pran tan
    time.sleep(0.1)
    return nimewo ** 2

def teste_sans_paralelizasyon():
    """
    Teste san paralelizasyon
    """
    print("=== SAN PARALELIZASYON ===")
    k√≤manse = time.time()
    
    rezilta = []
    for i in range(10):
        rezilta.append(kalkile_kare(i))
    
    fini = time.time()
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
    print(f"Tan pran: {fini - k√≤manse:.2f} segonn")

def teste_ak_threads():
    """
    Teste ak threads
    """
    print("=== AK THREADS ===")
    k√≤manse = time.time()
    
    threads = []
    rezilta = []
    
    def travay_thread(nimewo):
        rezilta.append(kalkile_kare(nimewo))
    
    for i in range(10):
        thread = threading.Thread(target=travay_thread, args=(i,))
        threads.append(thread)
        thread.start()
    
    for thread in threads:
        thread.join()
    
    fini = time.time()
    print(f"Rezilta: {rezilta}")
    print(f"Tan pran: {fini - k√≤manse:.2f} segonn")

def teste_ak_pwosesis():
    """
    Teste ak pwosesis
    """
    print("=== AK PWOSESIS ===")
    k√≤manse = time.time()
    
    pwosesis_yo = []
    rezilta = []
    
    def travay_pwosesis(nimewo):
        rezilta.append(kalkile_kare(nimewo))
    
    for i in range(10):
```
