    def ajoute_n√≤t(self, non, n√≤t):
        if non not in self.el√®v_yo:
            raise ValueError(f"El√®v {non} pa egziste")
        
        if not isinstance(n√≤t, (int, float)) or n√≤t < 0 or n√≤t > 20:
            raise ValueError("N√≤t dwe yon nimewo ant 0 ak 20")
        
        self.el√®v_yo[non]["n√≤t_yo"].append(n√≤t)
        print(f"N√≤t {n√≤t} ajoute pou {non}")
    
    def kalkile_mway√®n(self, non):
        if non not in self.el√®v_yo:
            raise ValueError(f"El√®v {non} pa egziste")
        
        n√≤t_yo = self.el√®v_yo[non]["n√≤t_yo"]
        if not n√≤t_yo:
            return 0
        
        return sum(n√≤t_yo) / len(n√≤t_yo)
    
    def jenera_rap√≤(self):
        print("\n=== RAP√í EL√àV YO ===")
        for non, enf√≤ in self.el√®v_yo.items():
            mway√®n = self.kalkile_mway√®n(non)
            print(f"{non}: {enf√≤['klas']}, Mway√®n: {mway√®n:.2f}")
    
    def sove_done(self):
        with open(self.fichier_done, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump(self.el√®v_yo, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
        print("Done sove ak siks√®")
    
    def chaje_done(self):
        try:
            with open(self.fichier_done, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                self.el√®v_yo = json.load(f)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.el√®v_yo = {}
    
    def eksp√≤t_csv(self, non_fichier):
        with open(non_fichier, "w", encoding="utf-8", newline="") as f:
            ekriv√® = csv.writer(f)
            ekriv√®.writerow(["Non", "Laj", "Klas", "Mway√®n"])
            
            for non, enf√≤ in self.el√®v_yo.items():
                mway√®n = self.kalkile_mway√®n(non)
                ekriv√®.writerow([non, enf√≤["laj"], enf√≤["klas"], f"{mway√®n:.2f}"])
        
        print(f"Rap√≤ eksp√≤te nan {non_fichier}")

# Fonksyon pou ent√®fas itilizat√®
def meni_prensipal():
    sist√®m = Sist√®mJesyonEl√®v()
    
    while True:
        print("\n=== MENI PRENSIPAL ===")
        print("1. Ajoute el√®v")
        print("2. Ajoute n√≤t")
        print("3. Kalkile mway√®n")
        print("4. Jenera rap√≤")
        print("5. Eksp√≤t CSV")
        print("6. Sove done")
        print("7. S√≤ti")
        
        chwa = input("Chwazi yon opsyon (1-7): ")
        
        try:
            if chwa == "1":
                non = input("Non el√®v: ")
                laj = int(input("Laj: "))
                klas = input("Klas: ")
                sist√®m.ajoute_el√®v(non, laj, klas)
            
            elif chwa == "2":
                non = input("Non el√®v: ")
                n√≤t = float(input("N√≤t: "))
                sist√®m.ajoute_n√≤t(non, n√≤t)
            
            elif chwa == "3":
                non = input("Non el√®v: ")
                mway√®n = sist√®m.kalkile_mway√®n(non)
                print(f"Mway√®n {non}: {mway√®n:.2f}")
            
            elif chwa == "4":
                sist√®m.jenera_rap√≤()
            
            elif chwa == "5":
                non_fichier = input("Non fichier CSV: ")
                sist√®m.eksp√≤t_csv(non_fichier)
            
            elif chwa == "6":
                sist√®m.sove_done()
            
            elif chwa == "7":
                sist√®m.sove_done()
                print("Orevwa!")
                break
            
            else:
                print("Chwa pa valab")
        
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Er√®: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    meni_prensipal()

## Appendiks A: Glos√®

### T√®m teknik yo

**Algorithm** - Yon seri enstriksyon pou rezoud yon pwobl√®m  
**API** - Application Programming Interface - Fason pwogram kominike  
**Array** - Yon koleksyon done √≤done  
**Boolean** - Kalite done ki gen s√®lman True oswa False  
**Class** - Mod√®l pou kreye obj√®  
**Compiler** - Pwogram ki konv√®ti k√≤d nan lang machin  
**Debugging** - Pwosesis pou jwenn ak korije er√®  
**Function** - Yon bl√≤k k√≤d ki f√® yon travay espesifik  
**IDE** - Integrated Development Environment - Zouti pou devlop√®  
**Library** - Yon koleksyon fonksyon ak klas  
**Loop** - Yon bl√≤k k√≤d ki repete  
**Method** - Fonksyon ki nan yon klas  
**Object** - Yon egzanp yon klas  
**Package** - Yon koleksyon modil  
**String** - Yon koleksyon karakt√® (t√®ks)  
**Variable** - Yon non pou yon val√® nan memwa
